if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: composer.json');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): composer.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('composer.json') != 'e27b9b9262034958574fb19dd02530046939d280') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('composer.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of composer.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== 'e27b9b9262034958574fb19dd02530046939d280') {
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== '6f9e10bbe60e87873b7d69ba4617a367e701ac79') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: composer.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('composer.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('composer.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('composer.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== 'e27b9b9262034958574fb19dd02530046939d280') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'c82dc747fae5d73692162b260320cb56d0dff9e3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c82dc747fae5d73692162b260320cb56d0dff9e3') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'd57d31666342d4554a1eb9a28d3ee5e05ab14f80') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'c82dc747fae5d73692162b260320cb56d0dff9e3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '6d2caa20ce890d266403ff471afd698b29fbe354') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '6d2caa20ce890d266403ff471afd698b29fbe354') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '851f1a764244762536a2cf18ef4af8e2075f8ad3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '6d2caa20ce890d266403ff471afd698b29fbe354') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf') != 'ca46f088620560c44dfa161582a9bab4da6cbb96') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== 'ca46f088620560c44dfa161582a9bab4da6cbb96') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== '036ec70355b29ad22e6cf87bc7f0e650d4055428') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf') !== 'ca46f088620560c44dfa161582a9bab4da6cbb96') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/danielmarschall/fileformats/filetypes.conf');
		}
	}
}

			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/licenses');
		}
	}
}
